jupyter@ictjupylblk01:~/gits/statsmed$ cat > /tmp/get_statsmed_stats.sh <<'STATSMED_EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

BASE="${BASE:-http://127.0.0.1:8000}"
OUT="/tmp/statsmed_public"
mkdir -p "$OUT"
rm -f "$OUT"/op_*.json "$OUT"/ids.txt

echo "Listing public operations from $BASE ..."
LIST="$(curl -sf "$BASE/api/quality/public")" || {
  echo "ERROR: cannot reach $BASE/api/quality/public" >&2
  exit 1
}
echo "$LIST" | jq -r '.[].id' > "$OUT/ids.txt"
N=$(wc -l < "$OUT/ids.txt" | tr -d ' ')
echo "Found $N public operations."

while read -r id; do
  [ -z "$id" ] && continue
  curl -sf "$BASE/api/quality/public/$id" > "$OUT/op_${id}.json"
done < "$OUT/ids.txt"

echo
echo "=== per-operation summary ==="
for f in "$OUT"/op_*.json; do
  jq -r '
    [.latest_run.results[]?
       | select(.chart_data.type | IN("laney_p_chart","laney_u_chart","laney_x_chart","i_mr_chart"))
    ] as $spc
    | [$spc[].chart_data.points[]?] as $pts
    | [$pts[] | select(.out_of_control == true)] as $ooc
    | "id=\(.id)\tname=\(.name)\tspc_charts=\($spc|length)\tpoints=\($pts|length)\tooc=\($ooc|length)"
  ' "$f"
done

echo
echo "=== global totals ==="
jq -s '
  [.[].latest_run.results[]?
     | select(.chart_data.type | IN("laney_p_chart","laney_u_chart","laney_x_chart","i_mr_chart"))
  ] as $spc
  | {
      spc_charts:     ($spc | length),
      points_total:   ([$spc[].chart_data.points[]?] | length),
      out_of_control: ([$spc[].chart_data.points[]? | select(.out_of_control == true)] | length)
    }
' "$OUT"/op_*.json

echo
echo "=== OOC vignette candidates ==="
for f in "$OUT"/op_*.json; do
bash /tmp/get_statsmed_stats.sh.chart_data.type)\t\(.date)"
Listing public operations from http://127.0.0.1:8000 ...
Found 11 public operations.

=== per-operation summary ===
id=10	name=Apollo Job Load	spc_charts=1	points=47	ooc=16
id=11	name=Examinations per Seniortime	spc_charts=5	points=190	ooc=4
id=12	name=DICOMcrawl per PACSTime	spc_charts=5	points=36	ooc=6
id=13	name=OmniScanPerformance	spc_charts=2	points=66	ooc=5
id=1	name=ICD10-Control	spc_charts=1	points=53	ooc=1
id=4	name=Examination Length	spc_charts=13	points=653	ooc=22
id=5	name=Report Times	spc_charts=8	points=488	ooc=29
id=6	name=Examinations per Writertime	spc_charts=5	points=190	ooc=3
id=7	name=Examinations per Scannertime	spc_charts=13	points=645	ooc=19
id=8	name=vLLM Apollo	spc_charts=2	points=6572	ooc=110
id=9	name=ApolloGPU Usage	spc_charts=11	points=9592	ooc=6398

=== global totals ===
{
  "spc_charts": 66,
  "points_total": 18532,
  "out_of_control": 6613
}
